\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l01801}01801\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}"{}"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l01802}01802\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ if\ self.nbins\ is\ None:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l01803}01803\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ return\ self.locs}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l01804}01804\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ step\ =\ max(int(np.ceil(len(self.locs)\ /\ self.nbins)),\ 1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l01805}01805\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ticks\ =\ self.locs[::step]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l01806}01806\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ for\ i\ in\ range(1,\ step):}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l01807}01807\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ticks1\ =\ self.locs[i::step]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l01808}01808\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ if\ np.abs(ticks1).min()\ <\ np.abs(ticks).min():}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l01960}01960\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ vmin\ -\/=\ self.\_offset}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l01961}01961\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ vmax\ -\/=\ self.\_offset}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l01962}01962\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ vmin\ =\ self.\_edge.ge(vmin)\ *\ step}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l01963}01963\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ n\ =\ (vmax\ -\/\ vmin\ +\ 0.001\ *\ step)\ //\ step}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l01964}01964\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ locs\ =\ vmin\ -\/\ step\ +\ np.arange(n\ +\ 3)\ *\ step\ +\ self.\_offset}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l01984}01984\ def\ scale\_range(vmin,\ vmax,\ n=1,\ threshold=100):}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l01985}01985\ \ \ \ \ dv\ =\ abs(vmax\ -\/\ vmin)\ \ \#\ >\ 0\ as\ nonsingular\ is\ called\ before.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02724}02724\ \ \ \ \ def\ \_\_call\_\_(self):}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02725}02725\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ vmin,\ vmax\ =\ self.axis.get\_view\_interval()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02726}02726\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ if\ (vmin\ *\ vmax)\ <\ 0\ and\ abs(1\ +\ vmax\ /\ vmin)\ <\ self.symthresh:}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02732}02732\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02733}\mbox{\hyperlink{classmatplotlib_1_1ticker_1_1AsinhLocator_a0a95f949dfcbad3ea6209bd22e92d611}{02733}}\ \ \ \ \ def\ tick\_values(self,\ vmin,\ vmax):}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02734}02734\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#\ Construct\ a\ set\ of\ uniformly-\/spaced\ "{}on-\/screen"{}\ locations.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02735}02735\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ymin,\ ymax\ =\ self.linear\_width\ *\ np.arcsinh(np.array([vmin,\ vmax])}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02736}02736\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ /\ self.linear\_width)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02737}02737\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ys\ =\ np.linspace(ymin,\ ymax,\ self.numticks)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02738}02738\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ zero\_dev\ =\ abs(ys\ /\ (ymax\ -\/\ ymin))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02739}02739\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ if\ ymin\ *\ ymax\ <\ 0:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02740}02740\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#\ Ensure\ that\ the\ zero\ tick-\/mark\ is\ included,\ if\ the\ axis\ straddles\ zero.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02741}02741\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ys\ =\ np.hstack([ys[(zero\_dev\ >\ 0.5\ /\ self.numticks)],\ 0.0])}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02742}02742\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02743}02743\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#\ Transform\ the\ "{}on-\/screen"{}\ grid\ to\ the\ data\ space:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02744}02744\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ xs\ =\ self.linear\_width\ *\ np.sinh(ys\ /\ self.linear\_width)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02745}02745\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ zero\_xs\ =\ (ys\ ==\ 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02746}02746\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02747}02747\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#\ Round\ the\ data-\/space\ values\ to\ be\ intuitive\ base-\/n\ numbers,\ keeping\ track\ of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02748}02748\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#\ positive\ and\ negative\ values\ separately\ and\ carefully\ treating\ the\ zero\ value.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02749}02749\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ with\ np.errstate(divide="{}ignore"{}):\ \ \#\ base\ **\ log(0)\ =\ base\ **\ -\/inf\ =\ 0.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02750}02750\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ if\ self.base\ >\ 1:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02751}02751\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ pows\ =\ (np.sign(xs)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02752}02752\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ *\ self.base\ **\ np.floor(np.log(abs(xs))\ /\ math.log(self.base)))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02753}02753\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ qs\ =\ np.outer(pows,\ self.subs).flatten()\ if\ self.subs\ else\ pows}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02754}02754\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ else:\ \ \#\ No\ need\ to\ adjust\ sign(pows),\ as\ it\ cancels\ out\ when\ computing\ qs.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02755}02755\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ pows\ =\ np.where(zero\_xs,\ 1,\ 10**np.floor(np.log10(abs(xs))))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02756}02756\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ qs\ =\ pows\ *\ np.round(xs\ /\ pows)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02757}02757\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ticks\ =\ np.array(sorted(set(qs)))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02758}02758\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02759}02759\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ return\ ticks\ if\ len(ticks)\ >=\ 2\ else\ np.linspace(vmin,\ vmax,\ self.numticks)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ticker_8py_source_l02760}02760\ }
